)@@G@@*[@@@@*SDFF*@A@@@@TABLE OF CONTENTS PROCESSOR, "TOC"  @^@@@@4GENERAL INFPJ
)@@G@@ORMATION    @G@@@@     TOC IS BASICALLY DESIGNED FOR USE ON THE UNISCOPEPK
)@@G@@ 100.  IT GIVES A @F@@@@ LISTING OF THE TABLE OF CONTENTS OF A PROGRAM FPL
)@@G@@ILE FORMATTED TO  @G@@@@ BETTER USE THE UNISCOPE SCREEN.  WHEREAS @PRT,TPM
)@@G@@ WILL GIVE THE ELEMENT  @G@@@@ TABLE OF A PROGRAM FILE, TOC CAN LIST THEPN
)@@G@@ ELEMENT TABLE, ENTRY POINT   @F@@@@ TABLE AND THE VARIOUS PROCEDURE TABPO
)@@G@@LES AS WELL.  TOC ALSO HAS THE@G@@@@ ADVANTAGEOUS FEATURE OF PAUSING WHEPP
)@@G@@N THE SCREEN BECOMES FULL TO ALLOW  @F@@@@ THE USER TO EXAMINE THE CONTEPQ
)@@G@@NTS OF THE SCREEN BEFORE PROCEEDING @G@@@@ TO THE REST OF THE TABLE BEINPR
)@@G@@G PRINTED.  IN ADDITION, THE USER MAY     @F@@@@ CHANGE OPTIONS OR TERMIPS
)@@G@@NATE EXECUTION WHENEVER TOC IS PAUSING FOR@ @@@@ A FULL SCREEN OF INFORMPT
)@@G@@ATION.@[@@@@0     @H@@@@     TOC DYNAMICALLY ASSIGNS AND FREES FILES AS PU
)@@G@@NECESSARY, AND WILL LEAVE     @F@@@@ THE USER'S FACILITIES EXACTLY AS THPV
)@@G@@EY WERE BEFORE EXECUTING TOC. @ @@@@4PROCESSOR CALLING SEQUENCE   @C@@@@PW
)@@G@@     TOC IS CALLED IN THE FOLLOWING MANNER:     @[@@@@SPACE @F@@@@0    *PX
)@@G@@********************************************************    @F@@@@0    *PY
)@@G@@                                                       *    @F@@@@0    *PZ
)@@G@@    @P*P.TOC[,OPTIONS] FILENAME.[ELTMASK][/VERMASK]    *    @F@@@@0    *QA
)@@G@@                                                       *    @F@@@@0    *QB
)@@G@@********************************************************    @]@@@@3FILE QC
)@@G@@NAME  @G@@@@      THE FILENAME MAY HAVE QUALIFIERS, F-CYCLES, AND/OR REAQD
)@@G@@D/WRITE     @G@@@@ KEYS IF THEY EXIST ON THE FILE.  THE EFFECT OF CALLINQE
)@@G@@G TOC WITHOUT     @F@@@@ OPTIONS IS TO GET THE SAME SORT OF LISTING PRODQF
)@@G@@UCED BY AN @PRT,T @F@@@@ BUT WITH DELETED ELEMENTS PRECEDED BY AN ASTERIQG
)@@G@@SK AND WITH THE   @G@@@@ LISTING FORMATTED TO BETTER UTILIZE THE UNISCOPQH
)@@G@@E SCREEN.  IF OMITTED,  @A@@@@ THE FILE NAME DEFAULTS TO "TPF$."  @A@@@@QI
)@@G@@3OPTIONAL ELEMENT/VERSION MASKS     @G@@@@     "ELTMASK" AND "VERMASK" AQJ
)@@G@@RE OPTIONAL 1-12 CHARACTER NAMES WHICH ARE@H@@@@ USED AS TESTS FOR PRINTQK
)@@G@@ING ENTRIES IN A TABLE.  IF "ELTMASK" IS PRESENT,     @G@@@@ TOC WILL PRQL
)@@G@@INT ONLY ENTRIES WHICH MASK SUCCESSFULLY WITH "ELTMASK".    @G@@@@ IN OTQM
)@@G@@HER WORDS, IF "ELTMASK" IS GIVEN AS "DA", TOC WILL ONLY PRINT     @F@@@@QN
)@@G@@ ENTRIES FROM THE SELECTED TABLE WHICH BEGIN WITH "DA".  THUS THE @G@@@@QO
)@@G@@ ELEMENTS (FOR EXAMPLE) "DA", "DA$$$", AND "DAVEY" WOULD ALL BE LISTED  QP
)@@G@@@F@@@@ IF "DA" WAS GIVEN AS "ELTMASK".  THIS MASK FEATURE WORKS WITH ANYQQ
)@@G@@@E@@@@ OF THE PROGRAM FILE'S TABLES, NOT JUST THE ELEMENT TABLE.  @[@@@@QR
)@@G@@0     @F@@@@     "VERMASK" FUNCTIONS WITH OR WITHOUT ALSO SPECIFYING "ELQS
)@@G@@TMASK"@F@@@@ BUT ONLY APPLIES TO THE ELEMENT TABLE SINCE ONLY ELEMENTS AQT
)@@G@@RE    @ @@@@ ALLOWED TO HAVE VERSIONS.    @]@@@@3OPTIONS    @#@@@@2AVAILQU
)@@G@@ABLE OPTIONS@B@@@@      THE OPTIONS AVAILABLE FOR TOC ARE:  @[@@@@SPACE QV
)@@G@@@F@@@@      B - BATCH MODE FORMAT.  TOC FORMATS THE OUTPUT TO FIT ON    QW
)@@G@@@F@@@@          THE PRINTER PAGE INSTEAD OF THE SCOPE SCREEN.  TOC DOES QX
)@@G@@@F@@@@          NOT PAUSE AFTER A FULL SCREEN BUT INSTEAD PROCEEDS TO   QY
)@@G@@@E@@@@          THE END OF THE TABLE BEING PRINTED AND STOPS.     @F@@@@QZ
)@@G@@          THIS OPTION IS IMPLEMENTED IF TOC IS CALLED IN A BATCH  @F@@@@RA
)@@G@@          RUN AND TAKES PRIORITY OVER ANY OTHER OPTION IF TOC IS  @E@@@@RB
)@@G@@          CALLED IN A DEMAND RUN.  THIS OPTION IS USEFUL FOR@E@@@@      RC
)@@G@@    GETTING A LISTING WHILE BREAKPOINTED AT THE SCOPE.@[@@@@SPACE @F@@@@RD
)@@G@@      E - ENTRY POINT TABLE.  TOC PRODUCES A LISTING OF THE FILE'S@G@@@@RE
)@@G@@          ENTRY POINT TABLE INSTEAD OF THE ELEMENT TABLE.  THE NAME     RF
)@@G@@@F@@@@          OF THE ENTRY POINT IS GIVEN, PRECEDED BY AN ASTERISK IF RG
)@@G@@@F@@@@          DELETED, AND FOLLOWED BY THE SEQUENCE NUMBER OF THE     RH
)@@G@@@B@@@@          ELEMENT IN WHICH IT OCCURS.     @[@@@@SPACE @G@@@@      RI
)@@G@@P - THIS SPECIFIES THAT THE ASSEMBLER PROCEDURE TABLE ENTRIES     @F@@@@RJ
)@@G@@          ARE TO BE PRINTED.  THE FORMAT IS THE SAME AS FOR THE   @ @@@@RK
)@@G@@          ENTRY POINT TABLE.  @[@@@@SPACE @F@@@@      F - THIS SPECIFIESRL
)@@G@@ THAT THE FORTRAN PROCEDURE TABLE ENTRIES @F@@@@          ARE TO BE PRINRM
)@@G@@TED IN THE SAME FORMAT AS THE ENTRY POINT @#@@@@          TABLE.  @[@@@@RN
)@@G@@SPACE @F@@@@      C - THIS OPTION SPECIFIES THAT THE COBOL PROCEDURE TABRO
)@@G@@LE    @F@@@@          ENTRIES ARE TO BE PRINTED.  AGAIN, THE ENTRY POINTRP
)@@G@@ TABLE@E@@@@          FORMAT IS USED, WITH ONE EXCEPTION.  IF THE COBOL RQ
)@@G@@@F@@@@          PROCEDURE NAME EXCEEDS 12 CHARACTERS, AN ASTERISK IS    RR
)@@G@@@F@@@@          APPENDED TO THE FIRST 12 CHARACTERS TO INDICATE THE     RS
)@@G@@@D@@@@          REMAINING PORTION OF THE NAME IS NOT LISTED.@[@@@@SPACE RT
)@@G@@@F@@@@ NOTE:  ALL THE ABOVE OPTIONS ARE IMPLEMENTED IN THE ORDER IN     RU
